毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到轮机工程领域复杂工程问题的恰当表述中。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate presentation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能针对轮机工程领域的系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。 Can establish a suitable mathematical model for a system or process in the field of marine engineering, and use appropriate boundary conditions to solve.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础、专业知识和数学模型分析、比较轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals expertise and mathematical model to the analysis and comparation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-1能够根据实际情况，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别轮机工程问题的影响因素。 Based on the real situation, be able to identify factors involved in the problems in marine engineering by using relevant scientific knowledge, together with desk research.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-2 能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立复杂轮机工程问题的模型，对问题进行描述。 Be able to describe the complicated problems and establish model for them by using principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，结合文献研究、案例教训和专家经验，对复杂轮机工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论和解决方案。 Be able to analyze complex marine engineering problems, draw reasonable conclusions and put forward solutions to them by comprehensive use of the principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science together with literature review, case study and application of expert experience.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-1 能够调查工程问题背景和需求，明确设计或开发目标。 Be able to analyze the background and requirements of engineering projects and define the design or development objectives.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-2能够按照国际公约、法规和标准，建立有效可行的设计方案，并依据设计方案对系统、单元或管理流程进行设计，并具有创新意识。 Be able to make up an effective and practical design in according with international conventions, regulations and standards, implement and figure out the system, unit or management process，with the sense of innovation.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-3 在设计和开发的各环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Take into consideration factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment in each step of design and development.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-1 能够按照科学原理，运用文献研究、访谈、案例探究等方法，进行复杂轮机工程问题解决方案的调研和分析。 Be capable of investigating and analyzing solutions to the complex marine engineering problems in the manner of desk study, interview, case study in line with scientific principle and theory.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-2 能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂轮机工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，进行实验并获取数据。 Be able to design the experimental plan, establish experimental system, carry out experiments and obtain data by  comprehensively using of scientific principles and methods for complex problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。 Be able to analyze and explicate obtained results from the experiments and draw reasonable and valid conclusions.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-1 了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂轮机工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具，并理解其局限性。 Have knowledge of the principle and application methods of modern tools, and be able to select and use appropriate technology, resources and modern information technology tools for marine engineering problems.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-2能够针对复杂机械工程问题，选择、使用或开发现代工程工具进行预测与模拟，并能够理解相关结果的局限性。 Be able to select, apply or develop modern engineering tools to predict and simulate sophisticated mechanical engineering problems, and understand the limitations of relevant results.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-1了解工程伦理基本内涵、轮机工程的发展历史、航海文化和国际公约、国内法规及行业规范。 Understand the general concepts of engineering ethics, and analyze and make judgement on the rationality of the projects based on the history of marine engineering, maritime culture, international conventions, domestic regulations and industry rules.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-2 能够理解轮机工程实践和复杂轮机工程问题对社会、健康、安全、法律的影响，理解应承担的责任。 Be able to understand the impact of marine engineering practice and projects on society, health, safety and law, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-1 能够理解我国及国际海事领域环境保护和社会可持续发展的政策、理念和内涵。 Be able to understand the policy, concept and connotation of environmental protection and social sustainable development in maritime field in China and worldwide.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-2能够具备在专业实践和社会实践中的情景意识，通过知识学习和工作实践经验，综合分析评价复杂轮机工程问题时对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。 Have awareness of environment and sustainable development in professional practice and social practice, and be able to comprehensively analyze and evaluate the impact of complex marine engineering projects on the environment and social sustainable development via knowledge learning and work experience.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-1 具有人文社会科学素养，践行社会主义核心价值观，树立正确的人生观和世界观。具有履行职责和规范所需的健康体魄和心理。 Have the quality of humanities and social sciences, respect the socialist core values, and establish a correct outlook on life and the world. Have excellent physique and psychology needed to perform the engineering duties and norms.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-2 熟知国际国内法规，维护国家形象，遵守轮机工程职业道德和职业规范。 Be familiar with international and domestic laws and regulations, maintain national image and abide by professional ethics and norms of marine engineering.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-3 熟知轮机工程对经济、民生和科学技术进步的贡献，增强职业荣誉感，积极履行责任。 Be familiar with the contribution of marine engineering to economy, people's livelihood and scientific and technological progress, safeguard professional honor and actively undertake responsibilities.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-1 具有团队协作意识，具有组织管理多学科背景下的团队的能力和自我管理能力。  With the sense of teamwork, be able to organize and manage the team under with the multi-disciplinary background and be self-discipline and self-management.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-2 具有团队精神，能够作为团队成员完成指定任务。 Be willing work in a team and able to accomplish assigned tasks as a team member.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-3具有领导能力，能够作为负责人组织团队完成指定的工作，并与团队成员有效沟通，共享信息。 Have the leadership capacity, be able to organize the team to complete the assigned work, and communicate effectively with team members and share information with them.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-1了解轮机工程专业领域的国内国际发展趋势、研究热点，能够以发言、讨论、工程图纸、撰写报告或论文的形式，与业界同行交流轮机工程专业领域的问题。 Understand the national and international development trend of the field of marine engineering, and be able to write professional papers, technical reports and design documents on marine engineering issues.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-2并具有国际视野，能够理解和尊重世界不同文化的差异性和多样性，能够使用公共英语和专业英语，与不同国家和地区的轮机工程相关人员进行口语、书面等跨文化沟通交流。 Have an international perspective, understand the distinguished features in marine engineering field，be able to use general English and professional English to communicate with marine engineers in different countries and regions in the oral and written forms.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-1理解工程管理的基本原理和经济学基本知识，掌握船舶建造运营和设备购置维修等全周期、全流程的成本构成。 Understand the basic knowledge of engineering management and economics related to engineering activities, master the cost structure of the whole cycle and the whole process of ship construction and operation and equipment purchase and maintenance.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-2能够在多学科环境下的项目管理过程中，针对轮机工程项目合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法 In the process of project management under multidisciplinary background, be able to apply the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods in marine engineering projects.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-1能在社会发展的大背景下，树立自主学习和终身学习意识，掌握自主学习的方式方法。 In the context of social development, establish the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-2掌握自主学习方法，针对轮机工程领域复杂工程，具备自主学习、提出问题、归纳总结等能力。 Master the method of independent learning, and have the ability to learn independently, ask questions, summarize and summarize for complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到轮机工程领域复杂工程问题的恰当表述中。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate presentation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能针对轮机工程领域的系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。 Can establish a suitable mathematical model for a system or process in the field of marine engineering, and use appropriate boundary conditions to solve.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础、专业知识和数学模型分析、比较轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals expertise and mathematical model to the analysis and comparation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-1能够根据实际情况，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别轮机工程问题的影响因素。 Based on the real situation, be able to identify factors involved in the problems in marine engineering by using relevant scientific knowledge, together with desk research.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-2 能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立复杂轮机工程问题的模型，对问题进行描述。 Be able to describe the complicated problems and establish model for them by using principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，结合文献研究、案例教训和专家经验，对复杂轮机工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论和解决方案。 Be able to analyze complex marine engineering problems, draw reasonable conclusions and put forward solutions to them by comprehensive use of the principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science together with literature review, case study and application of expert experience.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-1 能够调查工程问题背景和需求，明确设计或开发目标。 Be able to analyze the background and requirements of engineering projects and define the design or development objectives.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-2能够按照国际公约、法规和标准，建立有效可行的设计方案，并依据设计方案对系统、单元或管理流程进行设计，并具有创新意识。 Be able to make up an effective and practical design in according with international conventions, regulations and standards, implement and figure out the system, unit or management process，with the sense of innovation.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-3 在设计和开发的各环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Take into consideration factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment in each step of design and development.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-1 能够按照科学原理，运用文献研究、访谈、案例探究等方法，进行复杂轮机工程问题解决方案的调研和分析。 Be capable of investigating and analyzing solutions to the complex marine engineering problems in the manner of desk study, interview, case study in line with scientific principle and theory.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-2 能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂轮机工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，进行实验并获取数据。 Be able to design the experimental plan, establish experimental system, carry out experiments and obtain data by  comprehensively using of scientific principles and methods for complex problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。 Be able to analyze and explicate obtained results from the experiments and draw reasonable and valid conclusions.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-1 了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂轮机工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具，并理解其局限性。 Have knowledge of the principle and application methods of modern tools, and be able to select and use appropriate technology, resources and modern information technology tools for marine engineering problems.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-2能够针对复杂机械工程问题，选择、使用或开发现代工程工具进行预测与模拟，并能够理解相关结果的局限性。 Be able to select, apply or develop modern engineering tools to predict and simulate sophisticated mechanical engineering problems, and understand the limitations of relevant results.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-1了解工程伦理基本内涵、轮机工程的发展历史、航海文化和国际公约、国内法规及行业规范。 Understand the general concepts of engineering ethics, and analyze and make judgement on the rationality of the projects based on the history of marine engineering, maritime culture, international conventions, domestic regulations and industry rules.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-2 能够理解轮机工程实践和复杂轮机工程问题对社会、健康、安全、法律的影响，理解应承担的责任。 Be able to understand the impact of marine engineering practice and projects on society, health, safety and law, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-1 能够理解我国及国际海事领域环境保护和社会可持续发展的政策、理念和内涵。 Be able to understand the policy, concept and connotation of environmental protection and social sustainable development in maritime field in China and worldwide.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-2能够具备在专业实践和社会实践中的情景意识，通过知识学习和工作实践经验，综合分析评价复杂轮机工程问题时对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。 Have awareness of environment and sustainable development in professional practice and social practice, and be able to comprehensively analyze and evaluate the impact of complex marine engineering projects on the environment and social sustainable development via knowledge learning and work experience.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-1 具有人文社会科学素养，践行社会主义核心价值观，树立正确的人生观和世界观。具有履行职责和规范所需的健康体魄和心理。 Have the quality of humanities and social sciences, respect the socialist core values, and establish a correct outlook on life and the world. Have excellent physique and psychology needed to perform the engineering duties and norms.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-2 熟知国际国内法规，维护国家形象，遵守轮机工程职业道德和职业规范。 Be familiar with international and domestic laws and regulations, maintain national image and abide by professional ethics and norms of marine engineering.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-3 熟知轮机工程对经济、民生和科学技术进步的贡献，增强职业荣誉感，积极履行责任。 Be familiar with the contribution of marine engineering to economy, people's livelihood and scientific and technological progress, safeguard professional honor and actively undertake responsibilities.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-1 具有团队协作意识，具有组织管理多学科背景下的团队的能力和自我管理能力。  With the sense of teamwork, be able to organize and manage the team under with the multi-disciplinary background and be self-discipline and self-management.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-2 具有团队精神，能够作为团队成员完成指定任务。 Be willing work in a team and able to accomplish assigned tasks as a team member.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-3具有领导能力，能够作为负责人组织团队完成指定的工作，并与团队成员有效沟通，共享信息。 Have the leadership capacity, be able to organize the team to complete the assigned work, and communicate effectively with team members and share information with them.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-1了解轮机工程专业领域的国内国际发展趋势、研究热点，能够以发言、讨论、工程图纸、撰写报告或论文的形式，与业界同行交流轮机工程专业领域的问题。 Understand the national and international development trend of the field of marine engineering, and be able to write professional papers, technical reports and design documents on marine engineering issues.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-2并具有国际视野，能够理解和尊重世界不同文化的差异性和多样性，能够使用公共英语和专业英语，与不同国家和地区的轮机工程相关人员进行口语、书面等跨文化沟通交流。 Have an international perspective, understand the distinguished features in marine engineering field，be able to use general English and professional English to communicate with marine engineers in different countries and regions in the oral and written forms.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-1理解工程管理的基本原理和经济学基本知识，掌握船舶建造运营和设备购置维修等全周期、全流程的成本构成。 Understand the basic knowledge of engineering management and economics related to engineering activities, master the cost structure of the whole cycle and the whole process of ship construction and operation and equipment purchase and maintenance.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-2能够在多学科环境下的项目管理过程中，针对轮机工程项目合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法 In the process of project management under multidisciplinary background, be able to apply the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods in marine engineering projects.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-1能在社会发展的大背景下，树立自主学习和终身学习意识，掌握自主学习的方式方法。 In the context of social development, establish the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-2掌握自主学习方法，针对轮机工程领域复杂工程，具备自主学习、提出问题、归纳总结等能力。 Master the method of independent learning, and have the ability to learn independently, ask questions, summarize and summarize for complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到轮机工程领域复杂工程问题的恰当表述中。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate presentation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能针对轮机工程领域的系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。 Can establish a suitable mathematical model for a system or process in the field of marine engineering, and use appropriate boundary conditions to solve.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础、专业知识和数学模型分析、比较轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals expertise and mathematical model to the analysis and comparation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-1能够根据实际情况，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别轮机工程问题的影响因素。 Based on the real situation, be able to identify factors involved in the problems in marine engineering by using relevant scientific knowledge, together with desk research.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-2 能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立复杂轮机工程问题的模型，对问题进行描述。 Be able to describe the complicated problems and establish model for them by using principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，结合文献研究、案例教训和专家经验，对复杂轮机工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论和解决方案。 Be able to analyze complex marine engineering problems, draw reasonable conclusions and put forward solutions to them by comprehensive use of the principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science together with literature review, case study and application of expert experience.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-1 能够调查工程问题背景和需求，明确设计或开发目标。 Be able to analyze the background and requirements of engineering projects and define the design or development objectives.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-2能够按照国际公约、法规和标准，建立有效可行的设计方案，并依据设计方案对系统、单元或管理流程进行设计，并具有创新意识。 Be able to make up an effective and practical design in according with international conventions, regulations and standards, implement and figure out the system, unit or management process，with the sense of innovation.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-3 在设计和开发的各环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Take into consideration factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment in each step of design and development.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-1 能够按照科学原理，运用文献研究、访谈、案例探究等方法，进行复杂轮机工程问题解决方案的调研和分析。 Be capable of investigating and analyzing solutions to the complex marine engineering problems in the manner of desk study, interview, case study in line with scientific principle and theory.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-2 能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂轮机工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，进行实验并获取数据。 Be able to design the experimental plan, establish experimental system, carry out experiments and obtain data by  comprehensively using of scientific principles and methods for complex problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。 Be able to analyze and explicate obtained results from the experiments and draw reasonable and valid conclusions.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-1 了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂轮机工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具，并理解其局限性。 Have knowledge of the principle and application methods of modern tools, and be able to select and use appropriate technology, resources and modern information technology tools for marine engineering problems.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-2能够针对复杂机械工程问题，选择、使用或开发现代工程工具进行预测与模拟，并能够理解相关结果的局限性。 Be able to select, apply or develop modern engineering tools to predict and simulate sophisticated mechanical engineering problems, and understand the limitations of relevant results.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-1了解工程伦理基本内涵、轮机工程的发展历史、航海文化和国际公约、国内法规及行业规范。 Understand the general concepts of engineering ethics, and analyze and make judgement on the rationality of the projects based on the history of marine engineering, maritime culture, international conventions, domestic regulations and industry rules.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-2 能够理解轮机工程实践和复杂轮机工程问题对社会、健康、安全、法律的影响，理解应承担的责任。 Be able to understand the impact of marine engineering practice and projects on society, health, safety and law, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-1 能够理解我国及国际海事领域环境保护和社会可持续发展的政策、理念和内涵。 Be able to understand the policy, concept and connotation of environmental protection and social sustainable development in maritime field in China and worldwide.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-2能够具备在专业实践和社会实践中的情景意识，通过知识学习和工作实践经验，综合分析评价复杂轮机工程问题时对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。 Have awareness of environment and sustainable development in professional practice and social practice, and be able to comprehensively analyze and evaluate the impact of complex marine engineering projects on the environment and social sustainable development via knowledge learning and work experience.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-1 具有人文社会科学素养，践行社会主义核心价值观，树立正确的人生观和世界观。具有履行职责和规范所需的健康体魄和心理。 Have the quality of humanities and social sciences, respect the socialist core values, and establish a correct outlook on life and the world. Have excellent physique and psychology needed to perform the engineering duties and norms.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-2 熟知国际国内法规，维护国家形象，遵守轮机工程职业道德和职业规范。 Be familiar with international and domestic laws and regulations, maintain national image and abide by professional ethics and norms of marine engineering.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-3 熟知轮机工程对经济、民生和科学技术进步的贡献，增强职业荣誉感，积极履行责任。 Be familiar with the contribution of marine engineering to economy, people's livelihood and scientific and technological progress, safeguard professional honor and actively undertake responsibilities.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-1 具有团队协作意识，具有组织管理多学科背景下的团队的能力和自我管理能力。  With the sense of teamwork, be able to organize and manage the team under with the multi-disciplinary background and be self-discipline and self-management.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-2 具有团队精神，能够作为团队成员完成指定任务。 Be willing work in a team and able to accomplish assigned tasks as a team member.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-3具有领导能力，能够作为负责人组织团队完成指定的工作，并与团队成员有效沟通，共享信息。 Have the leadership capacity, be able to organize the team to complete the assigned work, and communicate effectively with team members and share information with them.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-1了解轮机工程专业领域的国内国际发展趋势、研究热点，能够以发言、讨论、工程图纸、撰写报告或论文的形式，与业界同行交流轮机工程专业领域的问题。 Understand the national and international development trend of the field of marine engineering, and be able to write professional papers, technical reports and design documents on marine engineering issues.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-2并具有国际视野，能够理解和尊重世界不同文化的差异性和多样性，能够使用公共英语和专业英语，与不同国家和地区的轮机工程相关人员进行口语、书面等跨文化沟通交流。 Have an international perspective, understand the distinguished features in marine engineering field，be able to use general English and professional English to communicate with marine engineers in different countries and regions in the oral and written forms.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-1理解工程管理的基本原理和经济学基本知识，掌握船舶建造运营和设备购置维修等全周期、全流程的成本构成。 Understand the basic knowledge of engineering management and economics related to engineering activities, master the cost structure of the whole cycle and the whole process of ship construction and operation and equipment purchase and maintenance.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-2能够在多学科环境下的项目管理过程中，针对轮机工程项目合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法 In the process of project management under multidisciplinary background, be able to apply the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods in marine engineering projects.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-1能在社会发展的大背景下，树立自主学习和终身学习意识，掌握自主学习的方式方法。 In the context of social development, establish the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-2掌握自主学习方法，针对轮机工程领域复杂工程，具备自主学习、提出问题、归纳总结等能力。 Master the method of independent learning, and have the ability to learn independently, ask questions, summarize and summarize for complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到轮机工程领域复杂工程问题的恰当表述中。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate presentation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能针对轮机工程领域的系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。 Can establish a suitable mathematical model for a system or process in the field of marine engineering, and use appropriate boundary conditions to solve.
毕业要求1 工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识用于解决轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 No.1Engineering knowledge Be able to apply knowledge of  mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.	能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础、专业知识和数学模型分析、比较轮机工程领域的复杂工程问题。 Ability to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals expertise and mathematical model to the analysis and comparation of complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-1能够根据实际情况，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别轮机工程问题的影响因素。 Based on the real situation, be able to identify factors involved in the problems in marine engineering by using relevant scientific knowledge, together with desk research.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-2 能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立复杂轮机工程问题的模型，对问题进行描述。 Be able to describe the complicated problems and establish model for them by using principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science.
毕业要求2 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，并获得有效结论。 No.2 Problem analysis Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to mark, express and analyze sophisticated problems in the field of marine engineering by using of reference and obtain resonable conclusions.	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，结合文献研究、案例教训和专家经验，对复杂轮机工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论和解决方案。 Be able to analyze complex marine engineering problems, draw reasonable conclusions and put forward solutions to them by comprehensive use of the principles and methods of mathematics, natural science and engineering science together with literature review, case study and application of expert experience.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-1 能够调查工程问题背景和需求，明确设计或开发目标。 Be able to analyze the background and requirements of engineering projects and define the design or development objectives.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-2能够按照国际公约、法规和标准，建立有效可行的设计方案，并依据设计方案对系统、单元或管理流程进行设计，并具有创新意识。 Be able to make up an effective and practical design in according with international conventions, regulations and standards, implement and figure out the system, unit or management process，with the sense of innovation.
毕业要求3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 No.3 Design/provide solutions Be able to design and put forward solutions to complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering, design systems, units (components) or technological processes that meet specific requirements, and present the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account  factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment, etc..	3-3 在设计和开发的各环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Take into consideration factors of society, health, safety, legislation, culture and environment in each step of design and development.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-1 能够按照科学原理，运用文献研究、访谈、案例探究等方法，进行复杂轮机工程问题解决方案的调研和分析。 Be capable of investigating and analyzing solutions to the complex marine engineering problems in the manner of desk study, interview, case study in line with scientific principle and theory.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-2 能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂轮机工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，进行实验并获取数据。 Be able to design the experimental plan, establish experimental system, carry out experiments and obtain data by  comprehensively using of scientific principles and methods for complex problems in the field of marine engineering.
毕业要求4 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 No.4 Study and research Be able to study complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering by means of scientific principles and scientific methods, such as experiments design, data analysis, and be able to draw reasonable and valid conclusions.	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。 Be able to analyze and explicate obtained results from the experiments and draw reasonable and valid conclusions.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-1 了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂轮机工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具，并理解其局限性。 Have knowledge of the principle and application methods of modern tools, and be able to select and use appropriate technology, resources and modern information technology tools for marine engineering problems.
毕业要求5 使用现代工具：能够针对轮机工程专业领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 No.5 Use of modern tools Be able to develop, select and apply appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology for the complex marine engineering problems, including prediction on and simulation of the problems, and understand the associated limitations.	5-2能够针对复杂机械工程问题，选择、使用或开发现代工程工具进行预测与模拟，并能够理解相关结果的局限性。 Be able to select, apply or develop modern engineering tools to predict and simulate sophisticated mechanical engineering problems, and understand the limitations of relevant results.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-1了解工程伦理基本内涵、轮机工程的发展历史、航海文化和国际公约、国内法规及行业规范。 Understand the general concepts of engineering ethics, and analyze and make judgement on the rationality of the projects based on the history of marine engineering, maritime culture, international conventions, domestic regulations and industry rules.
毕业要求6 工程与社会：能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 No.6 Engineering and society Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of the solution to the complicated engineering problems engineering and the professional engineering practice on on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.	6-2 能够理解轮机工程实践和复杂轮机工程问题对社会、健康、安全、法律的影响，理解应承担的责任。 Be able to understand the impact of marine engineering practice and projects on society, health, safety and law, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-1 能够理解我国及国际海事领域环境保护和社会可持续发展的政策、理念和内涵。 Be able to understand the policy, concept and connotation of environmental protection and social sustainable development in maritime field in China and worldwide.
毕业要求7 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对轮机工程专业领域内的复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 No.7 Environment and sustainable development Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of marine engineering practice of complicated projects   on the sustainable development of environment and Society in the field of marine engineering.	7-2能够具备在专业实践和社会实践中的情景意识，通过知识学习和工作实践经验，综合分析评价复杂轮机工程问题时对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。 Have awareness of environment and sustainable development in professional practice and social practice, and be able to comprehensively analyze and evaluate the impact of complex marine engineering projects on the environment and social sustainable development via knowledge learning and work experience.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-1 具有人文社会科学素养，践行社会主义核心价值观，树立正确的人生观和世界观。具有履行职责和规范所需的健康体魄和心理。 Have the quality of humanities and social sciences, respect the socialist core values, and establish a correct outlook on life and the world. Have excellent physique and psychology needed to perform the engineering duties and norms.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-2 熟知国际国内法规，维护国家形象，遵守轮机工程职业道德和职业规范。 Be familiar with international and domestic laws and regulations, maintain national image and abide by professional ethics and norms of marine engineering.
毕业要求8 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在轮机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 No.8 Professional norms With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in marine engineering practice, and fulfill the responsibilities.	8-3 熟知轮机工程对经济、民生和科学技术进步的贡献，增强职业荣誉感，积极履行责任。 Be familiar with the contribution of marine engineering to economy, people's livelihood and scientific and technological progress, safeguard professional honor and actively undertake responsibilities.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-1 具有团队协作意识，具有组织管理多学科背景下的团队的能力和自我管理能力。  With the sense of teamwork, be able to organize and manage the team under with the multi-disciplinary background and be self-discipline and self-management.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-2 具有团队精神，能够作为团队成员完成指定任务。 Be willing work in a team and able to accomplish assigned tasks as a team member.
毕业要求9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 No.9 Individual role and teamwork Be able to play the role of individual, team member and leader in a team with multi-disciplinary background.	9-3具有领导能力，能够作为负责人组织团队完成指定的工作，并与团队成员有效沟通，共享信息。 Have the leadership capacity, be able to organize the team to complete the assigned work, and communicate effectively with team members and share information with them.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-1了解轮机工程专业领域的国内国际发展趋势、研究热点，能够以发言、讨论、工程图纸、撰写报告或论文的形式，与业界同行交流轮机工程专业领域的问题。 Understand the national and international development trend of the field of marine engineering, and be able to write professional papers, technical reports and design documents on marine engineering issues.
毕业要求10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 No.10 Communication Be able to effectively communicate with peers in the industry and with the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and documents, making statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, and having a certain international horizon and be able to communicate  with others in a cross-cultural context.	10-2并具有国际视野，能够理解和尊重世界不同文化的差异性和多样性，能够使用公共英语和专业英语，与不同国家和地区的轮机工程相关人员进行口语、书面等跨文化沟通交流。 Have an international perspective, understand the distinguished features in marine engineering field，be able to use general English and professional English to communicate with marine engineers in different countries and regions in the oral and written forms.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-1理解工程管理的基本原理和经济学基本知识，掌握船舶建造运营和设备购置维修等全周期、全流程的成本构成。 Understand the basic knowledge of engineering management and economics related to engineering activities, master the cost structure of the whole cycle and the whole process of ship construction and operation and equipment purchase and maintenance.
毕业要求11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 No.11 Project management Understand and master the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods, and be able to apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-2能够在多学科环境下的项目管理过程中，针对轮机工程项目合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法 In the process of project management under multidisciplinary background, be able to apply the engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods in marine engineering projects.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-1能在社会发展的大背景下，树立自主学习和终身学习意识，掌握自主学习的方式方法。 In the context of social development, establish the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning.
毕业要求12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 No12 Lifelong learning Have the consciousness of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and the capacity to develop.	12-2掌握自主学习方法，针对轮机工程领域复杂工程，具备自主学习、提出问题、归纳总结等能力。 Master the method of independent learning, and have the ability to learn independently, ask questions, summarize and summarize for complex engineering problems in the field of marine engineering.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
